FreeBSD Ports: X11-wm
=====================

Search ports for: All Package Name Description Long description
Maintainer Requires

--------------

X Window System window managers.
~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~~

**\ `aewm-1.2.7\_4 <https://svnweb.FreeBSD.org/ports/head/x11-wm/aewm>`__**
    | ICCCM-compliant window manager based on 9wm
    | `Long
      description <https://svnweb.FreeBSD.org/ports/head/x11-wm/aewm/pkg-descr?revision=HEAD>`__

      \| `Main Web Site <http://www.red-bean.com/decklin/aewm/>`__

    | *Requires:*

      `libXext-1.3.3\_1,1 <x11.html#libXext-1.3.3_1,1>`__,
